If  an  individual,  fays  Grotius,  can  alienate  his

his  fubjeifts  the  public  tranquillity.  Be  it  fo  ;  I

On  monarchy.

HITHERTO  we  have  confidered  the

fonage  or  real  man  5  pofTefTed  of  the  right  of

ex-

iiS        A    TREATISE    ON    the

exerting  it  agreeable  to  the  laws.     Such  a  per*
fon  is  denominated  a  monarch  or  king.

In  other  adminiftrations  it  is  common  for  a

latter.

prince,  together  with  the  public  force  of  the

all  the  fprings  of  the  machine  are  in  the  fame

oppofite  motions  counteracting  and  deftroying

fpecies  of  government  in  which  the  leaft  effbrt
